name="references">\xd0\x9e\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8a\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85</a>\n\n  <a name="references--prefer-const"></a><a name="2.1"></a>\n  - [2.1](#references--prefer-const) \xd0\x98\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 `const` \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8a\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85; \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd1\x8f\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83\xd1\x8e \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b `Object.prototype`, \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83? \xd0\xad\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd1\x83\xd1\x82 \xd0\xb1\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb2 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd1\x85 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8a\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0, \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc `{ hasOwnProperty: false }`, \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 \xd1\x8d\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8a\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x82 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 \xd0\xb1\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c `null` (`Object.create(null)`).\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    console.log(object.hasOwnProperty(key));\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    console.log(Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(object, key));\n\n    // \xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd1\x87\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\n    const has = Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty; // \xd0\x9a\xd1\x8d\xd1\x88\xd0\xb8\xd1\x80\xd1\x83\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81 \xd0\xb2 \xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd1\x85 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd1\x83\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f.\n    console.log(has.call(object, key));\n    /* \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 */\n    import has from \'has\'; // https://www.npmjs.com/package/has\n    console.log(has(object, key));\n    ```\n\n  <a name="objects--rest-spread"></a>\n  - [3.8](#objects--rest-spread) \xd0\x98\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80 \xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x88\xd0\xb8\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe [`Object.assign`](https://developer.mozilla.org/ru/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Object/assign) \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x85\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb8\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8a\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2. \xd0\x98\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd1\x88\xd0\xb8\xd1\x85\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f \xd1\x81\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2, \xd1\x87\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x83\xd1\x87\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c \xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8a\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x82 \xd1\x81 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd1\x83\xd1\x89\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb8 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb8.\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8c \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    const original = { a: 1, b: 2 };\n    const copy = Object.assign(original, { c: 3 }); // \xd1\x8d\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb8\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 `original` \xe0\xb2\xa0_\xe0\xb2\xa0\n    delete copy.a; // \xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\n\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    const original = { a: 1, b: 2 };\n    const copy = Object.assign({}, original, { c: 3 }); // copy => { a: 1, b: 2, c: 3 }\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    const original = { a: 1, b: 2 };\n    const copy = { ...original, c: 3 }; // copy => { a: 1, b: 2, c: 3 }\n\n    const { a, ...noA } = copy; // noA => { b: 2, c: 3 }\n    ```\n\n**[\xe2\xac\x86 \xd0\xba \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8e](#\xd0\x9e\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5)**\n\n## <a name="arrays--callback-return"></a><a name="4.5"></a>\n  - [4.7](#arrays--callback-return) \xd0\x98\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b `return` \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbd\xd1\x83\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8 \xd1\x84\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb2 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x85 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0. \xd0\x9c\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb6\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd1\x83\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c `return`, \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe \xd1\x84\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82 \xd0\xb8\xd0\xb7 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd1\x83\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8, \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb2\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x89\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8e\xd1\x89\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb7 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85 \xd1\x8d\xd1\x84\xd1\x84\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2. [8.2](#arrows--implicit-return). eslint: [`array-callback-return`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/array-callback-return)\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    [1, 2, 3].map((x) => {\n      const y = x + 1;\n      return x * y;\n    });\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    [1, 2, 3].map((x) => x + 1);\n\n    // \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb1\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x83 \xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2. ([\xd0\x9e\xd0\xb1\xd1\x81\xd1\x83\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5](https://github.com/airbnb/javascript/issues/794))\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    function foo() {\n      // ...\n    }\n\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    const foo = function () {\n      // ...\n    };\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    // \xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8f, \xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd1\x87\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x82 \xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9(-\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85) \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9(-\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85)\n    const foo = function uniqueMoreDescriptiveLexicalFoo() {\n      // ...\n    };\n    ```\n\n  <a name="functions--iife"></a><a name="7.2"></a>\n  - [7.2](#functions--iife) \xd0\x9e\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x87\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb2 \xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x84\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8. eslint: [`wrap-iife`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/wrap-iife.html)\n\n    > \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83? \xd0\x9d\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f \xd1\x84\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba. \xd0\xa7\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8b \xd1\x87\xd1\x91\xd1\x82\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c \xd1\x8d\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe \xe2\x80\x94 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x84\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8e \xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8e\xd1\x89\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb2 \xd0\xb5\xd1\x89\xd1\x91 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8 \xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8. \xd0\x9e\xd0\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5, \xd1\x87\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb2 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb8\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x81 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd1\x83\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd1\x88\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbd\xd1\x83\xd0\xb6\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x84\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8.\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\x9d\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f \xd1\x84\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\n    (function () {\n      console.log(\'Welcome to the Internet. \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 `\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba` \xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba \xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba \xd0\x9d\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x80 `arguments`. \xd0\x9e\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb1\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x83\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f \xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\x9d\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 `arguments`, \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe \xd1\x8d\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2 `...`. eslint: [`prefer-rest-params`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/prefer-rest-params)\n\n    > \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83? `...` \xd1\x8f\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82 \xd0\xbe \xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc, \xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb3\xd1\x83\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb8\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd1\x87\xd1\x8c. \xd0\x9a\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe, \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x91\xd1\x82 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x8f\xd1\x89\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2, \xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8a\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x82 \xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba `arguments`.\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    function concatenateAll() {\n      const args = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments);\n      return args.join(\'\');\n    }\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    function concatenateAll(...args) {\n      return args.join(\'\');\n    }\n    ```\n\n  <a handleThings(opts) {\n      // \xd0\x9d\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82! \xd0\x9c\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb6\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b   // \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb2\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5: \xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f opts \xd0\xb1\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 \xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb6\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9,\n      // \xd0\x9e\xd1\x82\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x88\xd0\xb8\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f `...` \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd1\x84\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8. eslint: [`prefer-spread`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/prefer-spread)\n\n    > \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83? \xd0\xad\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe \xd1\x87\xd0\xb8\xd1\x89\xd0\xb5, \xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbd\xd1\x83\xd0\xb6\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x81\xd1\x82, \xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c `new` \xd1\x81 `apply`.\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    const x = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];\n    console.log.apply(console, x);\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    const x = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];\n    console.log(...x);\n\n    // 5]);\n    ```\n\n  <a name="functions--signature-invocation-indentation"></a>\n  - [7.15](#functions--signature-invocation-indentation) \xd0\xa4\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8 \xd1\x80\xd1\x83\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5: \xd1\x81 \xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc \xd1\x8d\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5, \xd1\x81 \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbf\xd1\x8f\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xb2 \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd1\x86\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x8d\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0. eslint: [`function-paren-newline`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/function-paren-newline)\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    function foo(bar,\n                 baz,\n                 quux) {\n      // ...\n    }\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    function foo(\n      bar,\n      baz,\n      quux,\n    ) {\n      // ...\n    }\n\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    console.log(foo,\n      bar,\n      baz);\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    console.log(\n      foo,\n      bar,\n      baz,\n    );\n    ```\n\n**[\xe2\xac\x86 \xd0\xba \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8e](#\xd0\x9e\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5)**\n\n## <a name="arrows--use-them"></a><a name="8.1"></a>\n  - [8.1](#arrows--use-them) \xd0\x9a\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc  ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    [1, 2, 3].map(function (x) {\n      const y = x + 1;\n      return x * y;\n    });\n\n    // [`arrow-body-style`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/arrow-body-style.html)\n\n    > \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83? \xd0\xa1\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb9 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd1\x85\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80. \xd0\x9a\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe \xd1\x84\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb9 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5, \xd1\x82\xd0\xbe \xd1\x8d\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbb\xd1\x83\xd1\x87\xd1\x88\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x87\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f.\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    [1, 2, return `A string containing the ${nextNumber}.`;\n    });\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    [1, 2, 3].map((number, index) => ({\n      [index]: number,\n    }));\n\n    // \xd0\x9d\xd0\xb5\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb2\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82 \xd1\x81 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb8 let bool = false;\n\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    foo(() => bool = true);\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    foo(() => {\n      bool = true;\n \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x87\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb3\xd1\x83\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd1\x8f\xd1\x81\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb8 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8. eslint: [`arrow-parens`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/arrow-parens.html)\n    > \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83? \xd0\x9c\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb8\xd1\x80\xd1\x83\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 \xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd1\x87\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8 \xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb3\xd1\x83\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b.\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    [1, 2, 3].map(x => x * x);\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    [1, 2, 3].map((x) => x * x);\n\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    [1, 2, 3].map(number => (\n      `A long string with the ${number}. 1;\n      return x * y;\n    });\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    [1, 2, 3].map((x) => {\n      const y = x + 1;\n      return x * y;\n    });\n    ```\n\n  <a name="arrows--confusing"></a><a name="8.5"></a>\n  - [8.5](#arrows--confusing) \xd0\x98\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x81\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8 \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd1\x84\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8 (`=>`) \xd1\x81 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb8 \xd1\x81\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f (`<=`, `>=`). eslint: [`no-confusing-arrow`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-confusing-arrow)\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    const itemHeight = (item) => item.height <= 256 ? item.largeSize : item.smallSize;\n\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    const itemHeight = (item) => item.height >= 256 ? item.largeSize : item.smallSize;\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    const itemHeight = (item) => (item.height <= 256 ? item.largeSize : item.smallSize);\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    const itemHeight = (item) => {\n      const { height, largeSize, smallSize } = item;\n      return height <= 256 ? largeSize : smallSize;\n    };\n    ```\n\n  <a name="whitespace--implicit-arrow-linebreak"></a>\n  - [8.6](#whitespace--implicit-arrow-linebreak) \xd0\x97\xd0\xb0\xd1\x84\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd1\x80\xd1\x83\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 [`implicit-arrow-linebreak`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/implicit-arrow-linebreak)\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    (foo) =>\n      bar;\n    (foo) =>\n    this.queue.splice(0, 1);\n      return value;\n    };\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    class Queue {\n      constructor(contents = []) {\n        this.queue = \xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd1\x91\xd1\x82 \xd0\xba \xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb1\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5.\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    class Foo {\n      bar() { return 1; }\n      bar() { return 2; }\n    }\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    class Foo {\n (`import`/`export`) \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd1\x83\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc. \xd0\x92\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4 \xd0\xb2 \xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd1\x88\xd1\x83 \xd0\xbb\xd1\x8e\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83\xd1\x8e \xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd1\x83\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xbd\xd1\x83\xd1\x8e \xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83.\n\n    > \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83? \xd0\x9c\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd1\x83\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 \xe2\x80\x94 \xd1\x8d\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb1\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd1\x83\xd1\x89\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb5. \xd0\x94\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x87\xd0\xbd\xd1\x91\xd0\xbc \xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb9\xd1\x87\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81!\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    const AirbnbStyleGuide = require(\'./AirbnbStyleGuide\');\n \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb6\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8a\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc.\n\n    ```javascript\n    const numbers = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5];\n\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    let sum = 0;\n    for (let num of numbers) {\n      sum += num;\n    }\n    sum === 15;\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    let sum = 0;\n    numbers.forEach((num) => {\n      sum += num;\n    });\n    sum === 15;\n\n    // \xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd1\x87\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe (\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd1\x83 \xd1\x84\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb9)\n    const sum = numbers.reduce((total, num) => total + num, 0);\n    sum === 15;\n\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    const increasedByOne = [];\n    for (let i = 0; i < numbers.length; i++) {\n      increasedByOne.push(numbers[i] + 1);\n    }\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    const increasedByOne = [];\n    numbers.forEach((num) => {\n      increasedByOne.push(num + 1);\n    });\n\n    // \xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd1\x87\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe (\xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb2 \xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb4\xd1\x83\xd1\x85\xd0\xb5)\n    const increasedByOne = numbers.map((num) => num + 1);\n    ```\n\n  <a name="generators--nope"></a><a name="11.2"></a>\n  - [11.2](#generators--nope) \xd0\x9d\xd0\xb5 [11.3](#generators--spacing) \xd0\x95\xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd1\x91-\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c \xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b, \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 [\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x88 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82](#generators--nope), \xd1\x83\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x8c, \xd1\x87\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe `*` \xd1\x83 \xd1\x84\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb3\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb6\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc. eslint: [`generator-star-spacing`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/generator-star-spacing)\n\n    > \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83? `function` \xd0\xb8 `*` \xd1\x8f\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f\xd1\x8e\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f \xd1\x87\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c\xd1\x8e \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb8 \xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xba\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8e\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0. `*` \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x8f\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd1\x84\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f `function`, `function*` \xd1\x8f\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f \xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd1\x83\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb9, \xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd1\x87\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x82 `function`.\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    function * foo() {\n      // ...\n    }\n\n    const bar = function * () {\n      // ...\n    };\n\n    const baz = function *() {\n      // ...\n    };\n\n    const quux = function*() {\n      // ...\n    };\n\n    function*foo() {\n      // ...\n    }\n\n    function *foo() {\n      // ...\n    }\n\n    // \xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8c \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    function\n    *\n    foo() {\n      // ...\n    }\n\n    const wat = function\n    *\n    () {\n      // ...\n    };\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    function* foo() {\n      // ...\n    }\n\n    const foo = function* () {\n      // ...\n    };\n    ```\n\n**[\xe2\xac\x86 \xd0\xba \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8e](#\xd0\x9e\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5)**\n\n## <a name="properties">\xd0\xa1\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0</a>\n\n  <a name="properties--dot"></a><a name="12.1"></a>\n  - [12.1](#properties--dot) \xd0\x98\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd1\x87\xd0\xbd\xd1\x83\xd1\x8e \xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8e \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x83\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xba \xd1\x81\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc. eslint: [`dot-notation`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/dot-notation.html)\n\n    ```javascript\n    const luke = {\n      jedi: true,\n      age: 28,\n    };\n\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    const isJedi = luke[\'jedi\'];\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    const isJedi = luke.jedi;\n    ```\n\n  <a name="properties--bracket"></a><a name="12.2"></a>\n  - [12.2](#properties--bracket) \xd0\x98\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xbd\xd1\x83\xd1\x8e \xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8e `[]`, \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x85\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb2 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9.\n\n    ```javascript\n    const luke = {\n      jedi: true,\n      age: 28,\n    };\n\n    function getProp(prop) {\n      return luke[prop];\n    }\n\n    const isJedi = getProp(\'jedi\');\n    ```\n\n  <a name="es2016-properties--exponentiation-operator"></a>\n  - [12.3](#es2016-properties--exponentiation-operator) \xd0\x98\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80 `**` \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb2 \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8c. eslint: [`no-restricted-properties`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-restricted-properties).\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    const binary = Math.pow(2, 10);\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    const binary = 2 ** 10;\n    ```\n\n**[\xe2\xac\x86 \xd0\xba \xd0\x92\xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 `const` \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 `let` \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8a\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85. \xd0\x9d\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x8d\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8e \xd0\xb3\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85. \xd0\x9d\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb8\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb3\xd1\x80\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb3\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd1\x91\xd0\xbd. eslint: [`no-undef`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-undef) [`prefer-const`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/prefer-const)\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    superPower = new SuperPower();\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    const superPower = new SuperPower();\n    ```\n\n  <a name="variables--one-const"></a><a name="13.2"></a>\n  - [13.2](#variables--one-const) \xd0\x98\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8a\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 `const` \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 `let` \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f \xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 [`one-var`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/one-var.html)\n\n    > \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83? \xd0\xa2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x89\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c \xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb5. \xd0\xa2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb1\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbe \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x89\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8 `;` \xd0\xb8 `,` \xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb8\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd1\x8c \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe \xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8a\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8e \xd1\x81 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd1\x89\xd1\x8c\xd1\x8e \xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd1\x87\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0, \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe \xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe, \xd1\x87\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c \xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb7 \xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x81\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83.\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    const items = getItems(),\n        goSportsTeam = true,\n        dragonball = \'z\';\n\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    // \xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd1\x8c \xd0\xb3\xd1\x80\xd1\x83\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb8\xd1\x80\xd1\x83\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 `const`, \xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc `let`.\n\n    > \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83? \xd0\xad\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe, \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb2 \xd0\xb1\xd1\x83\xd0\xb4\xd1\x83\xd1\x89\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc \xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd1\x83\xd1\x8e, \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83\xd1\x8e \xd0\xbe\xd1\x82 \xd0\xb7\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb9. \xd0\xa2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb5 ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n\n    const array = [1, 2, 3];\n    let num = 1;\n    num++;\n    --num;\n\n    let sum = 0;\n    let truthyCount = 0;\n    for (let i = 0; i < array.length; i++) {\n      let value = array[i];\n      sum += value;\n      if (value) {\n        truthyCount++;\n      }\n    }\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n\n // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    const foo = \'superLongLongLongLongLongLongLongLongString\';\n    ```\n\n  <a name="variables--no-unused-vars"></a>\n  - [13.8](#variables--no-unused-vars) \xd0\x97\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c eslint: [`no-unused-vars`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-unused-vars)\n\n    > \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83? \xd0\x9f\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb5, \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb5     console.log(\'anonymous function expression\');\n      };\n    }\n    ```\n\n  <a name="hoisting--named-expressions"></a><a name="hoisting--named-expressions"></a><a name="14.3"></a>\n  - [14.3](#hoisting--named-expressions) \xd0\x94\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85 \xd1\x84\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85 \xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x85 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9, \xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe \xd1\x84\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8.\n\n    ```javascript\n    function example() {\n      console.log(named); // => undefined\n\n      named(); // => TypeError named \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x8f\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f \xd1\x84\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb9\n\n      superPower(); // => ReferenceError superPower \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\n\n      var named = function superPower() {\n        console.log(\'Flying\');\n      };\n    }\n\n    // \xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x81\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe, \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8f \xd1\x84\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8\n    // \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 \xd1\x81 \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9.\n    function example() {\n      console.log(named); // => undefined\n\n      named(); // => TypeError named \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x8f\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f \xd1\x84\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb9\n\n      var named = function named() {\n        console.log(\'named\');\n      };\n    }\n    ```\n\n  <a name="hoisting--declarations"></a><a name="14.4"></a>\n  - [14.4](#hoisting--declarations) \xd0\x9f\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8a\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8 \xd1\x84\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb5\xd1\x91 \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb8 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8e\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x85 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8.\n\n    ```javascript\n    function example() {\n      superPower(); name="comparison-operators--equality">\xd0\x9e\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd1\x81\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb8 \xd0\x98\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 `===` \xd0\xb8 `!==` \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe `==` \xd0\xb8 `!=`. eslint: \xd0\xa3\xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b, \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba `if`, \xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b\xd1\x87\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f\xd1\x8e\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbf\xd1\x83\xd1\x82\xd1\x91\xd0\xbc \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xba \xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb8\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbf\xd1\x83 `Boolean` \xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb7 \xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4 `ToBoolean` \xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd1\x83\xd1\x8e\xd1\x82 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd1\x83\xd1\x8e\xd1\x89\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc:\n    - **Object** \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd1\x83\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 **true**\n    - **Undefined** \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd1\x83\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 **false**\n    - **Null** \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd1\x83\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 **false**\n    - **Boolean** \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd1\x83\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 **\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8e \xd0\xb1\xd1\x83\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb0**\n    - **Number** \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd1\x83\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 **false**, \xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 **+0, -0, or NaN**, \xd0\xb2 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd1\x83\xd1\x87\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f\xd1\x85 **true**\n    - **String** \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd1\x83\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 **false**, \xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbf\xd1\x83\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f `\'\'`, \xd0\xb2 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd1\x83\xd1\x87\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f\xd1\x85 **true**\n\n    ```javascript\n    if ([0] && []) {\n      // true\n      // \xd0\x9c\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2 (\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbf\xd1\x83\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9) \xd1\x8f\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8a\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc, \xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8a\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb2\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x89\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8e\xd1\x82 true\n    }\n    ```\n\n  <a name="comparison--shortcuts"></a><a name="15.3"></a>\n  - [15.3](#comparison--shortcuts) \xd0\x98\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbd\xd1\x83\xd1\x8e \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x84\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8e \xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb6\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe  - [15.5](#comparison--switch-blocks) \xd0\x98\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x84\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb3\xd1\x83\xd1\x80\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f `case` \xd0\xb8 `default`, \xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82 \xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8 (\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80, `let`, `const`, `function`, \xd0\xb8 `class`). eslint: [`no-case-declarations`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-case-declarations.html).\n\n    > \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83? \xd0\x9b\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x81\xd0\xb8\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc `switch` \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5, \xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb8\xd1\x80\xd1\x83\xd1\x8e\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f \xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8, \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82 \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb2\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb2 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba `case`. \xd0\x92\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8e\xd1\x82 \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x8b, \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbc\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe `case` \xd0\xbf\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8e\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb8 \xd1\x82\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5.\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    switch (foo) {\n      case 1:\n        let x = 1;\n        break;\n      case 2:\n        const y = 2;\n        break;\n      case 3:\n        function f() {\n          // ...\n        }\n        break;\n      default:\n        class C {}\n    }\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    switch (foo) {\n      case 1: {\n        let x = 1;\n        break;\n      }\n      case 2: {\n        const y = 2;\n        break;\n      }\n      case 3: {\n        function f() {\n          // ...\n        }\n        break;\n      }\n      case 4:\n        bar();\n        break;\n      default: {\n        class C {}\n      }\n    }\n    ```\n\n  <a name="comparison--nested-ternaries"></a><a name="15.6"></a>\n  - [15.6](#comparison--nested-ternaries) \xd0\xa2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb6\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb1\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb2 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd1\x88\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd1\x83\xd1\x87\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb2 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb6\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b \xd0\xb1\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c \xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5. eslint: [`no-nested-ternary`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-nested-ternary.html).\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    const foo = maybe1 > maybe2\n      ? "bar"\n      : value1 > value2 ? "baz" : null;\n\n    // \xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85 \xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f\n    const maybeNull = value1 > value2 ? \'baz\' : null;\n\n    const foo = maybe1 > maybe2\n      ? \'bar\'\n      : maybeNull;\n\n    // \xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd1\x87\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\n    const foo = maybe1 > maybe2 ? \'bar\' : maybeNull;\n    ```\n\n  <a name="comparison--unneeded-ternary"></a><a name="15.7"></a>\n  - [15.7](#comparison--unneeded-ternary) \xd0\x98\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd1\x83\xd0\xb6\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2. eslint: [`no-unneeded-ternary`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-unneeded-ternary.html).\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    const foo = a ? a : b;\n    const bar = c ? true : false;\n    const baz = c ? false : true;\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    const foo = a || b;\n    const bar = !!c;\n    const baz = !c;\n    ```\n\n  <a name="comparison--no-mixed-operators"></a>\n  - [15.8](#comparison--no-mixed-operators) \xd0\x9f\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x88\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2, \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x89\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb8\xd1\x85 \xd0\xb2 \xd0\xba\xd1\x80\xd1\x83\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8. \xd0\x95\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc \xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8e\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc \xd1\x8f\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f\xd1\x8e\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd1\x84\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b: `+`, `-` \xd0\xb8 `**`, \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba \xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba \xd0\xb8\xd1\x85 \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 \xd1\x88\xd0\xb8\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb8\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd. \xd0\x9c\xd1\x8b \xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd1\x83\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8e\xd1\x87\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c `/` \xd0\xb8 `*` \xd0\xb2 \xd0\xba\xd1\x80\xd1\x83\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8, \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xba\xd1\x83 \xd0\xb8\xd1\x85 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x87\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc, \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x88\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8e\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f. eslint: [`no-mixed-operators`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-mixed-operators.html)\n\n    > \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83? \xd0\xad\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe \xd1\x83\xd0\xbb\xd1\x83\xd1\x87\xd1\x88\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 \xd1\x87\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c \xd0\xb8 \xd1\x83\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd1\x87\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0.\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    const foo = a && b < 0 || c > 0 || d + 1 === 0;\n\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    const bar = a ** b - 5 % d;\n\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    // \xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb6\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f, \xd0\xb4\xd1\x83\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f \xd1\x87\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe \xd1\x8d\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe (a || b) && c\n    if (a || b && c) {\n      return d;\n    }\n\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    const bar = a + b / c * d;\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    const foo = (a && b < 0) || c > 0 || (d + 1 === 0);\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    const bar = a ** b - (5 % d);\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    if (a || (b && c)) {\n      return d;\n    }\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    const bar = a + (b / c) * d;\n    ```\n\n**[\xe2\xac\x86 \xd0\xba name="blocks">\xd0\x91\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8</a>\n\n  <a name="blocks--braces"></a><a name="16.1"></a>\n  - [16.1](#blocks--braces) \xd0\x98\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x84\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb3\xd1\x83\xd1\x80\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8, \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba. eslint: [`nonblock-statement-body-position`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/nonblock-statement-body-position)\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    if (test)\n      return false;\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    if (test) return false;\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    if (test) {\n      return false;\n    }\n\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    function foo() { return false; }\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    function bar() {\n      return false;\n    }\n    ```\n\n  <a name="blocks--cuddled-elses"></a><a name="16.2"></a>\n  - [16.2](#blocks--cuddled-elses) \xd0\x95\xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb2 \xd1\x83\xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb8 `if` \xd0\xb8 `else` \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8e\xd1\x82 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba, \xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80 `else` \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5, \xd0\xb3\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8e\xd1\x89\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f \xd1\x84\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb3\xd1\x83\xd1\x80\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f \xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0 `if`. eslint: [`brace-style`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/brace-style.html)\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    if (test) {\n      thing1();\n      thing2();\n    }\n    else {\n      thing3();\n    }\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    if (test) {\n      thing1();\n      thing2();\n    } else {\n      thing3();\n    }\n    ```\n\n  <a name="blocks--no-else-return"></a><a name="16.3"></a>\n  - [16.3](#blocks--no-else-return) \xd0\x95\xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb2 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba\xd0\xb5 `if` \xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb2\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80 `return`, \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd1\x83\xd1\x8e\xd1\x89\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba `else` \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbd\xd1\x83\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd. `return`  \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbd\xd1\x83\xd1\x82\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0 `else if`, \xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd1\x83\xd1\x8e\xd1\x89\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc \xd0\xb7\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc `if`, \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb9 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82 `return`, \xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 \xd0\xb1\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c \xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd1\x91\xd0\xbd \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2 `if`. eslint: [`no-else-return`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-else-return)\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    function foo() {\n      if (x) {\n        return x;\n      } else {\n        return y;\n      }\n    }\n\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    function cats() {\n      if (x) {\n        return x;\n      } else if (y) {\n        return y;\n      }\n    }\n\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    function dogs() {\n      if (x) {\n        return x;\n      } else {\n        if (y) {\n          return y;\n        }\n      }\n    }\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    function foo() {\n      if (x) {\n        return x;\n      }\n\n      return y;\n    }\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    function cats() {\n      if (x) {\n        return x;\n      }\n\n      if (y) {\n        return y;\n      }\n    }\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    function dogs(x) {\n      if (x) {\n        if (z) {\n          return y;\n        }\n      } else {\n        return z;\n      }\n    }\n    ```\n\n**[\xe2\xac\x86 \xd0\xba \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8e](#\xd0\x9e\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5)**\n\n## <a name="control-statements">\xd0\xa3\xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f\xd1\x8e\xd1\x89\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b</a>\n\n  <a name="control-statements"></a>\n  - [17.1](#control-statements) \xd0\x95\xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd1\x88 \xd1\x83\xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f\xd1\x8e\xd1\x89\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80 (`if`, `while` \xd0\xb8 \xd1\x82.\xd0\xb4.) \xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd1\x88\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 name="coercion--numbers"></a><a name="21.3"></a>\n  - [22.3](#coercion--numbers) \xd0\xa7\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0: \xd0\x98\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 `Number` \xd0\xb8 `parseInt` \xd1\x81   ```javascript\n    const inputValue = \'4\';\n\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    const val = new Number(inputValue);\n\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    const \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb7\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xba \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8e (\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80, \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f `DOM` \xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5-\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb5 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f, \xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba `Backbone` \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f), \xd0\xbf\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8a\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0 (\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb8\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xb9 \xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba \xc2\xab\xd1\x85\xd1\x8d\xd1\x88\xc2\xbb) \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb7\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f. \xd0\xad\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 \xd0\xb4\xd1\x80\xd1\x83\xd0\xb3\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc \xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb7\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd1\x87\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c \xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd1\x88\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85 \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb7 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xb8 \xd0\xb8\xd0\xb7\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f \xd0\xba\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb4\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd1\x87\xd0\xb8\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8b\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f. \xd0\x9a \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd1\x83, \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe:\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    $(this).trigger(\'listingUpdated\', listing.id);\n\n    // ...\n\n    $(this).on(\'listingUpdated\', (e, listingID) => {\n      // \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 ```javascript\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    $(this).trigger(\'listingUpdated\', { listingID: listing.id });\n\n    // ...\n\n    $(this).on(\'listingUpdated\', (e, data) => {\n      // \xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb5\xd1\x82 \xd1\x87\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe-\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe \xd1\x81 data.listingID\n    });\n    ```\n\n**[\xe2\xac\x86 \xd0\xba \xd1\x85\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8f\xd1\x89\xd0\xb8\xd1\x85 \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x8a\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd1\x82 jQuery, \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb7\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0 `$`.\n\n \xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8e](#\xd0\x9e\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5)**\n\n## <a name="standard-library">\xd0\xa1\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0</a>\n\n  [\xd0\xa1\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd1\x82\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb1\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb1\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5\xd0\xba\xd0\xb0](https://developer.mozilla.org/ru/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects)\n  \xd1\x81\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb6\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82 \xd1\x83\xd1\x82\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x8b, \xd1\x84\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd1\x8c \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd1\x8b\xd1\x85 \xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0, \xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8 \xd0\xbe\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd1\x8c \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd1\x80\xd0\xb6\xd0\xba\xd0\xb8 \xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb0.\n\n  <a name="standard-library--isnan"></a>\n  - [29.1](#standard-library--isnan) \xd0\x98\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 `Number.isNaN` \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe \xd0\xb3\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe `isNaN`.\n    eslint: [`no-restricted-globals`](https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-restricted-globals)\n\n    > \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83? \xd0\x93\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f \xd1\x84\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f `isNaN` \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5-\xd1\x87\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xba \xd1\x87\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc, \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb2\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x89\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f `true` \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe, \xd1\x87\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f \xd0\xba `NaN`.\n    > \xd0\x95\xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe, \xd1\x81\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd1\x8f\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc.\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    isNaN(\'1.2\'); // false\n    isNaN(\'1.2.3\'); // true\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    Number.isNaN(\'1.2.3\'); // false\n    Number.isNaN(Number(\'1.2.3\')); // true\n    ```\n\n  <a name="standard-library--isfinite"></a>\n  - [29.2](#standard-library--isfinite) \xd0\x98\xd1\x81\xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xb7\xd1\x83\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 `Number.isFinite` \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbc\xd0\xb5\xd1\x81\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe > \xd0\x9f\xd0\xbe\xd1\x87\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83? \xd0\x93\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8c\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f \xd1\x84\xd1\x83\xd0\xbd\xd0\xba\xd1\x86\xd0\xb8\xd1\x8f `isFinite` \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5-\xd1\x87\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0 \xd0\xba \xd1\x87\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xbc, \xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb7\xd0\xb2\xd1\x80\xd0\xb0\xd1\x89\xd0\xb0\xd1\x8f `true` \xd0\xb4\xd0\xbb\xd1\x8f \xd0\xb2\xd1\x81\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe, \xd1\x87\xd1\x82\xd0\xbe \xd0\xbf\xd1\x80\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd1\x82\xd1\x81\xd1\x8f \xd0\xba \xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd1\x87\xd0\xbd\xd0\xbe\xd0\xbc\xd1\x83 \xd1\x87\xd0\xb8\xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd1\x83.\n    > \xd0\x95\xd1\x81\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb8 \xd1\x82\xd0\xb0\xd0\xba\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb2\xd0\xb5\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbd\xd0\xb8\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xbd\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb1\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb8\xd0\xbc\xd0\xbe, \xd1\x81\xd0\xb4\xd0\xb5\xd0\xbb\xd0\xb0\xd0\xb9\xd1\x82\xd0\xb5 \xd0\xb5\xd0\xb3\xd0\xbe \xd1\x8f\xd0\xb2\xd0\xbd\xd1\x8b\xd0\xbc.\n\n    ```javascript\n    // \xd0\xbf\xd0\xbb\xd0\xbe\xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\n    isFinite(\'2e3\'); // true\n\n    // \xd1\x85\xd0\xbe\xd1\x80\xd0\xbe\xd1\x88\xd0\xbe\n    Number.isFinite(\'2e3\'); // false\n    Number.isFinite(parseInt(\'2e3\', 10)); // true\n    ```\n\n**[\xe2\xac\x86 \xd0\xba
